2. Websocket for get financial data

2.1 Websocket connection
```
wss://data.tradingview.com/socket.io/websocket?type=chart
```

2.2 first message 
```
~m~55~m~{"m":"chart_create_session","p":["cs_GjT6ydCPZLC7",""]}
```

2.3 second message
```
~m~116~m~{"m":"resolve_symbol","p":["cs_GjT6ydCPZLC7","sds_sym_1","={\"adjustment\":\"splits\",\"symbol\":\"NASDAQ:NVDA\"}"]}
```

2.4 third message
```
~m~82~m~{"m":"create_series","p":["cs_GjT6ydCPZLC7","sds_1","s1","sds_sym_1","1W",300,""]}
```
